      15              : //======================================================================
      16              : //
      17              : // ecc_pm_sequencer.sv
      18              : // --------
      19              : // ECC point multiplication sequencer for the Secp384.
      20              : // 1) Point Addition (PA) and Point Doubling (PD) are based on 
      21              : //    "Complete Addition Formulas for Prime Order Elliptic Curves"
      22              : //    by Renes et. al. (Algorithm 1)
      23              : // 2) Modular Inversion (mod p, mod q) is based on "Fermat's little 
      24              : //    theorem (FLT)" implemented by exponentiation by squaring methos 
      25              : //    with window size of 3 bits.
      26              : // 3) All modular operations are performed in Montgomery domain.
      27              : //    mod p are modular operation respect to PRIME of SECP384 curve.
      28              : //    mod q are modular operation respect to GROUP ORDER of SECP384 curve.
      29              : // 4) To validate the given public key, we compare YY = Y^2 with 
      30              : //    RHS = X^3 + A X + B.
      31              : //
      32              : //======================================================================
      33              : 
      34              : module ecc_pm_sequencer 
      35              :     import ecc_pm_uop_pkg::*;
      36              :     #(
      37              :     parameter ADDR_WIDTH = 10,
      38              :     parameter DATA_WIDTH = 32
      39              :     )

      41       507518 :     input  wire                      clka,
      42           15 :     input  wire                      reset_n,
      43            6 :     input  wire                      zeroize,
      44            3 :     input  wire                      ena,
      45            0 :     input  wire  [ADDR_WIDTH-1 : 0]  addra,
      46            0 :     output logic [DATA_WIDTH-1 : 0]  douta
      47              :     );
